<Text>I ordered a table case for my 2001 table. They didn't have the original case but sent one that would fit my table.  Customer service was very good and the case came within a week.  My only problem is that I liked the original case better.  The pocket for the bolster was vertical and had separate pockets for sheets and other items.  The new one has one pocket which the bolster slides in horizontally and you have to put the sheets and other items on top of that.  Also, the original case's zippers went down to the bottom which made putting in the folded table easy.  The new zippers don't go down to the bottom and you have to lift the table and insert it in just right in order to zip up the case.

I just bought an Earthlite Massage Chair and am pleased with it so far.  The carrying case could be a little bigger so if you don't collapse the chair just right, it will still fit around the chair.

My table has lasted 14 years!!!  I hope my chair does, too!
-Miles of smiles :-) :-) :-)

<name>Classique Salon< /name>< review>
We ordered our "spirit" table from Earthlite. It did arrive quickly. As we set it up we noticed that the legs have to be extended carefully as there is no support (unlike a much cheaper table we have)connecting the two legs from either end with each other, thus there is a risk of breaking part of the table if you do not hold both legs, one in each hand and move them simultaneously. As soon as we set it up and tested it out, one of the bed supports snapped. We called Earhtlite and left a message to which we never got a response. I called back and talked to someone who said it would be forwarded on and I should expect a call back. We did not get a return call so I called again. I explained my dilemma and this time they forwarded me on to one of their associates. I explained the situation and how we had clients booked expecting to have this additional table. Earthlite seemed indifferent to my plight and the fact that we had to call and move clients. We had to wait five days to get a replacement despite them being 5 hours away.
The Sierra Comfort table we had first is not as wide but seems just as sturdy and comfortable yet cost 1/5th the price.</review>

I'm disappointed. The elastic band of the new massage chair replacement cover is quite snug and when the seat cover is placed over the seat, it looks absolutely perfect - just like in the picture. BUT, when you sit on it and work on your client/patient and get up again, the back side has pulled up a bit and the seat cover gets wrinkly and looks dumb and messy. Not just a little bit - it's quite obvious. I've pulled it back many times now, and even tried overcompensating for the sliding by really making it as tight as possible in the back, but it creeps creeping up and looks stupid. The elastic band should probably be a drawstring as I want to make it way tighter than the band can do by itself. I might bring in some thread and try tightening the bottom band more if possible (it might tear?). Or maybe I'll try stapling it on with a powerful stapler. I would have rather purchased the whole base with the seat cover stapled to the bottom for $50 or whatever because this is just dumb. I don't have time for this.< /Review>

<rate>5</rate>< text>
I purchased my first table from you about twenty years ago. It was in perfect condition when I sold after fifteen years prior to my world traveling adventures. Now settled down again with a new set of clients, of course my choice was EarthLite.

Being pretty disappointed in, yet understanding of, the disguise of free shipping, I'll advise this company to make more bold the fine print that speaks of exclusions to that coupon.

An even greater disappointment was the promise of a three-business-day delivery. This important lesson taught me to wait to schedule clients until products arrive! Over the course of the next eight days, my trips to the post office twenty minutes away only led to further disgust because of the seemingly missing table. Low and behold, a voicemail finally comes from Fed-Ex stating the package had been there for about a week. How was I to know Fed-Ex didn't deliver to post offices? I wish I knew that piece of apparently common knowledge. This information needed to be posted in bold font when purchasing on-line!

And now for the great news...EarthLite agreed! They refunded the expensive shipping costs, and they even said 'thank you' for bringing this to their attention. Each of the customer service department members I had the pleasure of politely whining to was kind, patient, and willing to listen and take action.
Good going, EarthLite!</text>

< review>
My dog has chronic allergies. We must have spent a couple thousand dollars on him under the care of Banfield in Petsmart and no matter what they put him on, from $90 dog food to countless medications. Not to  mention the many hours sitting in the room waiting to be seen.

Then I brought him to Ark. We didn't have to wait long like we normally do at Banfield. Dr Costuma evaluated him then took the time to discuss his conditions and  treatment. We were sent home with some antibiotics and a couple other medications. What a night and day difference! We have our old dog back. He's no longer miserable and chewing himself raw.

He'll probably be on medication to keep him itch free for the rest of his life (he's almost 9), but it's a small (and affordable) price to pay for his comfort.< /review>

<rating>5<//rating>< Text>
I wanted something in the area that was quick, not too busy, and affordable. I also wanted a place to work where i wont be bothered by the noise or the crowd. This was a great choice when I came across this plaza. I didnt want to spend too much, but still get fed enough that i wouldnt get hungry again during my way home.

Their gender neutral restrooms are located at the back of the establishment just past the condiments. There is plenty of parking, and lots of space to sit and dine. I sat by the windows at the high chairs and tables.

What really got me to like this place was their lunch special is actually ongoing - although it says lunch, it goes on all day - so you get a pretty good deal on a slice of pizza, a half sandwich and a salad or any 2 or 3 combinations of the latter. Then you can add a fountain drink for a buck more.< /Text>
